[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m issue was detected during fuzz testing of the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ThreeDXMLParser` component. The Jazzer sanitizer flagged an attempted outbound [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconnection to `jazzer.com:[0m[1;36m443[0m[39m`, indicating that untrusted XML input can trigger [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marbitrary network requests.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Overview  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During a fuzzing session, the parser received crafted input that caused the XML [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing logic to initiate an HTTPS connection to an external host [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`jazzer.com:[0m[1;36m443[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Jazzer’s SSRF sanitizer [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.ServerSideRequestForgery`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m intercepted [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis behavior and raised a `FuzzerSecurityIssueMedium` alert.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The issue is identified as an SSRF [0m[1;39m([0m[39mServer Side Request Forgery[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m vulnerability, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhere untrusted data influences the destination of network requests, potentially [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexposing or exfiltrating internal data or services.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The exception stack trace shows the SSRF check triggering in the [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ServerSideRequestForgery.checkSsrf` method.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The outbound request originates from standard Java networking classes [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`Socket.connect`, `HttpsURLConnectionImpl.getInputStream`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The XML parser [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`com.sun.org.apache.xerces.internal.impl.XMLEntityManager`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolves an external entity, causing the network call.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The parser under test is `org.apache.tika.parser.threedxml.ThreeDXMLParser`, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifically within the methods:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `parseRoot`  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `processZip`  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `parseContent`  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzz harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ThreeDXMLParserFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m invokes `parseOne`, which in turn [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdrives the SAX-based XML parsing path that leads to the SSRF.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Affected Code Areas for Investigation  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. **ThreeDXMLParser.java**  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – `parseRoot`, `processZip`, and `parseContent` to see how external entities [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor URIs are handled.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. **XML Entity Resolution**  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – The Xerces `XMLDocumentFragmentScannerImpl` and `XMLEntityManager` classes, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich perform entity resolution during parsing.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. **Network Connection Logic**  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – Standard Java networking paths [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`Socket.connect`, `HttpClient.openServer`, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`HttpsURLConnectionImpl.getInputStream`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to trace how untrusted URIs propagate into[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msocket creation.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. **SSRFSanitizer**  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – `ServerSideRequestForgery.checkSsrfSocket` to understand what patterns or [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata trigger the detection.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35morg.apache.tika.parser.threedxml.ThreeDXMLParser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mThreeDXMLParser.jav[0m[1;92ma:86[0m[1;39m)[0m     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcom.example.ThreeDXMLParserFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[39mThreeDXMLParserFuzzer.jav[0m[1;92ma:39[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEDUP_TOKEN: f8a914f52bb68598[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer-based fuzzer flagged a Server-Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in the [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThreeDXMLParser when it attempted to resolve external entities over HTTPS. To [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmitigate, a patch was proposed that configures the SAXParserFactory to disable [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal entity loading and enable secure processing. After applying the patch, the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuild failed with compilation errors: the added `[0m[1;35mfactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` calls [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrow `ParserConfigurationException`, which are neither caught nor declared, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcausing four unreported-exception errors in ThreeDXMLParser.java.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A Jazzer security sanitizer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ServerSideRequestForgery`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m detected an SSRF risk[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile the fuzzer invoked ThreeDXMLParser through [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ThreeDXMLParserFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The stack trace shows the parser calling into the JDK’s HTTPS URL handling via[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`HttpURLConnection.getInputStream`, triggered by Xerces XML parsing of external [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentities.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Jazzer classified the issue as a medium-severity FuzzerSecurityIssue: [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted data led to an outbound connection attempt to `jazzer.com:[0m[1;36m443[0m[39m`.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Observations in the Initial Issue  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The vulnerability arises from the default XML parser configuration, which [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallows external general entities, parameter entities, and external DTDs to be [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfetched over the network.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The crash input context is an XML document inside a ZIP archive [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe ThreeDXML[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformat[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, parsed by `ThreeDXMLParser.parseContent`.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The harness code [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ThreeDXMLParserFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m simply delegates to [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ThreeDXMLParser.parseOne`, so the root cause lives in the parser configuration.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - File modified:  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `tika-parsers-standard-modules/tika-parser-cad-module/src/main/java/org/apache[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m/tika/parser/threedxml/ThreeDXMLParser.java`  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add import:  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `import javax.xml.XMLConstants;`  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After creating the SAXParserFactory [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`factory = [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, insert:  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mfactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[39mXMLConstants.FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING, true[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mfactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http://xml.org/sax/features/external-general-entities"[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfalse[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mfactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http://xml.org/sax/features/external-parameter-entities"[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfalse[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mfactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http://apache.org/xml/features/nonvalidating/load-external[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m-dtd"[0m[39m, false[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The intent is to harden the parser against XXE/SSRF by disabling external [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentity resolution and enabling secure processing.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Patch Result and Compilation Errors  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Build failure in module `tika-parser-cad-module`:  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     unreported exception javax.xml.parsers.ParserConfigurationException; must be [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcaught or declared to be thrown[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       at ThreeDXMLParser.java:[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m132[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m27[0m[1;39m][0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       at ThreeDXMLParser.java:[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m133[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m27[0m[1;39m][0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       at ThreeDXMLParser.java:[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m134[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m27[0m[1;39m][0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       at ThreeDXMLParser.java:[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m135[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m27[0m[1;39m][0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Each `[0m[1;35mfactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call can throw a checked [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ParserConfigurationException` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand possibly `SAXNotRecognizedException` or [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`SAXNotSupportedException`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but the surrounding code does not handle or declare [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthese exceptions.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - As a result, the Java compiler rejects the patch.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Areas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - ThreeDXMLParser.java: review exception handling around `SAXParserFactory` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfiguration and parser instantiation. The method currently catches/parses other [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexceptions but not `ParserConfigurationException` at the feature-configuration [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstep.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Method signature of `parseRoot` [0m[35m/[0m[39m `parseContent` in ThreeDXMLParser: check [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeclared thrown exceptions to see if `ParserConfigurationException` can be [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpropagated.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other Tika modules that perform XML parsing: ensure consistent secure-feature [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfiguration and proper exception handling when disabling external entities.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Build configuration for `tika-parser-cad-module`: verify whether existing [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtry/catch blocks can be extended or method signatures updated to declare the new [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecked exceptions.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
